Nous consultons r\u00e9guli\u00e8rement des experts en suicide et automutilation pour soutenir nos politiques et leur mise en application et collaborer avec des organisations du monde entier pour assister les personnes en d\u00e9tresse.\n     \nBien qu\u2019il ne soit pas permis de glorifier ou de promouvoir volontairement ou non l\u2019automutilation ou le suicide, nous autorisons les discussions sur ce sujet, parce que nous souhaitons faire de Facebook un espace o\u00f9 chacun peut partager ses exp\u00e9riences, sensibiliser \u00e0 ces fl\u00e9aux et rechercher un soutien mutuel.\n  \nNous d\u00e9finissons l\u2019automutilation comme le fait de se blesser le corps de mani\u00e8re directe et volontaire, ce qui peut notamment s\u2019exprimer sous forme de blessures superficielles ou de troubles de l\u2019alimentation. Nous supprimons tout contenu qui encourage le suicide ou l\u2019automutilation, y compris le contenu fictif comme les m\u00e8mes ou illustrations et tout contenu explicite d\u2019automutilation, peu importe le contexte. Nous supprimons aussi le contenu qui identifie et cible n\u00e9gativement des victimes ou survivants d\u2019une tentative de suicide ou d\u2019une automutilation, que ce soit s\u00e9rieusement ou de mani\u00e8re humoristique ou rh\u00e9torique, ainsi que les images en temps r\u00e9el de suicide ou d\u2019automutilation. Le contenu sur le r\u00e9tablissement apr\u00e8s une tentative de suicide ou une automutilation qui est autoris\u00e9, mais peut contenir des images potentiellement d\u00e9rangeantes, est plac\u00e9 derri\u00e8re un \u00e9cran de sensibilit\u00e9.\n  \nLorsque des personnes publient ou recherchent du contenu li\u00e9 au suicide ou \u00e0 l\u2019automutilation, nous les redirigerons vers les organisations locales qui peuvent apporter un soutien \u00e0 une personne qui pr\u00e9sente un risque imminent d\u2019automutilation, nous contacterons les services d\u2019urgence locaux pour leur venir en aide.\n  \nConcernant le contenu en direct, les experts nous ont indiqu\u00e9 que si une personne d\u00e9clarait qu\u2019elle avait l\u2019intention de faire une tentative de suicide sur un streaming en direct, nous devrions conserver le contenu aussi longtemps que possible, car plus une personne parle devant une cam\u00e9ra, plus il y a de chances qu\u2019un ami ou un membre de sa famille appelle les services d\u2019urgence.\n  \nCependant, pour minimiser le risque d\u2019un impact n\u00e9gatif sur des tiers \u00e0 la suite du visionnage de ce contenu, nous stopperons le streaming en direct au moment o\u00f9 la menace devient une tentative. Comme indiqu\u00e9 ci-dessus, nous contacterons dans tous les cas les services d\u2019urgence si nous identifions qu\u2019une personne pr\u00e9sente un risque imminent de se faire du mal.\n  \n     \n Nous ne tol\u00e9rons pas ce type de comportement, car il emp\u00eache les gens de se sentir respect\u00e9s et en s\u00e9curit\u00e9 sur Facebook.  \n\n Nous distinguons les personnalit\u00e9s publiques des personnes priv\u00e9es, car notre plate-forme pr\u00f4ne l\u2019\u00e9change, ce qui implique souvent des commentaires critiques concernant des individus qui attirent l\u2019attention des m\u00e9dias ou du grand public. Concernant les personnalit\u00e9s publiques, nous supprimons les attaques graves et certaines attaques qui identifient directement la personnalit\u00e9 publique dans une publication ou un commentaire. Concernant les personnes priv\u00e9es, notre protection est plus large\u00a0: nous supprimons le contenu visant \u00e0 rabaisser une personne ou \u00e0 la couvrir de honte, et, notamment, les d\u00e9clarations relatives aux activit\u00e9s sexuelles de quelqu\u2019un. Nous reconnaissons que l\u2019intimidation et le harc\u00e8lement peuvent avoir des r\u00e9percussions \u00e9motionnelles plus graves pour les mineurs. C\u2019est pourquoi nos politiques offrent une protection plus \u00e9lev\u00e9e pour les utilisateurs \u00e2g\u00e9s de 13\u00a0\u00e0 18\u00a0ans. \n\n Le contexte et l\u2019intention importent\u00a0; nous autorisons les personnes \u00e0 publier et partager des publications si le contenu vise clairement \u00e0 condamner l\u2019intimidation et le harc\u00e8lement ou \u00e0 attirer l\u2019attention sur ces comportements. Dans certains cas, nous demandons que la personne cibl\u00e9e fasse elle-m\u00eame le signalement, car cela nous permet de savoir qu\u2019elle se sent intimid\u00e9e et harcel\u00e9e. En plus de signaler de tels comportements et contenus, nous encourageons les gens \u00e0 utiliser  les outils disponibles sur Facebook  pour se prot\u00e9ger contre ceux-ci. \n    \n     Nous avons \u00e9galement une  plate-forme de pr\u00e9vention contre l\u2019intimidation , qui est une ressource destin\u00e9e aux adolescents, aux parents et aux \u00e9ducateurs cherchant un soutien pour les questions li\u00e9es \u00e0 l\u2019intimidation et \u00e0 d\u2019autres conflits. Elle offre des conseils pas \u00e0 pas, y compris des informations sur la mani\u00e8re d\u2019ouvrir des discussions importantes concernant l\u2019intimidation. Apprenez-en davantage sur les mesures que nous prenons pour prot\u00e9ger les gens contre le harc\u00e8lement et l\u2019intimidation  ici . \n   \n "},"human_exploitation":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Ne publiez pas\u00a0: \n    \n      Du contenu (ou n\u2019adoptez pas de comportement) pouvant conduire \u00e0 l\u2019exploitation des personnes, notamment sous les formes suivantes\u00a0:\n\n      \n        Exploitation sexuelle des mineurs et des adultes \n        Vente d\u2019enfants \u00e0 des fins d\u2019adoption ill\u00e9gale\n         \n        Exploitation dans des orphelinats et    Trafic d\u2019organes ne se r\u00e9g\u00e9n\u00e9rant pas \n        Activit\u00e9s criminelles forc\u00e9es (par ex.\u00a0: mendicit\u00e9 forc\u00e9e, trafic de drogue forc\u00e9) \n        Recrutement d\u2019enfants soldats \n           \n\n      Du contenu favorisant\u00a0:\n      \n        Le recrutement de victimes potentielles par la force, la fraude, la contrainte, la sollicitation, la tromperie, le chantage ou autres actes non consentis \n        La contribution \u00e0 l\u2019exploitation des personnes en organisant, transportant, transf\u00e9rant, dissimulant ou n\u00e9gociant des victimes avant ou pendant leur exploitation  \n        L\u2019exploitant des humains en glorifiant, d\u00e9peignant ou pr\u00f4nant sa pratique \n        \n      Du contenu proposant d\u2019assurer le passage clandestin de personnes ou d\u2019y contribuer \n      \n         \n    \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   Apr\u00e8s avoir consult\u00e9 des sp\u00e9cialistes externes du monde entier, nous r\u00e9unissons plusieurs politiques concernant l\u2019exploitation, qui \u00e9taient jusqu\u2019\u00e0 pr\u00e9sent r\u00e9parties dans diff\u00e9rentes sections des Standards de la communaut\u00e9, pour n\u2019en former qu\u2019une\u00a0: elle sera centr\u00e9e sur l\u2019exploitation des personnes et abordera un grand nombre de pratiques n\u00e9fastes pouvant se manifester sur notre plate-forme. Ces sp\u00e9cialistes regroupent ces probl\u00e9matiques sous une appellation commune\u00a0: l\u2019exploitation des personnes.   \n     \n     \n     \n      Pour emp\u00eacher et r\u00e9duire ces pratiques, nous supprimons le contenu qui contribue \u00e0 l\u2019exploitation des personnes ou la coordonne, notamment la traite des personnes. Nous d\u00e9finissons la traite des personnes comme une activit\u00e9 privant un individu de sa libert\u00e9 pour en tirer profit. Il s\u2019agit d\u2019exploiter une personne pour la contraindre \u00e0 la    prostitution, au travail forc\u00e9 ou \u00e0 d\u2019autres activit\u00e9s contre son gr\u00e9. Elle fonctionne par la tromperie, la force et la contrainte, et avilit les individus en les privant de leur libert\u00e9 pour le profit \u00e9conomique ou mat\u00e9riel d\u2019autres personnes.   \n     \n     \n     \n      La traite des personnes touche le monde entier et prend de nombreuses formes\u00a0; elle peut toucher tous les humains, quels que soient leur \u00e2ge, leurs origines socio\u00e9conomiques, leur ethnie, leur genre et leur lieu de vie. Elle prend de nombreux visages, et tous les types de traite peuvent prendre diff\u00e9rentes ampleurs. En raison de la nature contraignante de cette maltraitance, les victimes ne sont pas consentantes. \n     \n     \n     \n      Bien que nous prenions soin de faire la distinction entre traite des personnes et passage clandestin, ces deux pratiques peuvent \u00eatre associ\u00e9es et se recouper. Les Nations Unies d\u00e9finissent le passage clandestin des personnes comme le fait de permettre ou d\u2019assurer l\u2019entr\u00e9e ill\u00e9gale dans un pays en traversant une fronti\u00e8re internationale. Sans qu\u2019il soit fait appel \u00e0 la contrainte ou \u00e0 la force, il peut tout de m\u00eame aboutir \u00e0 l\u2019exploitation de personnes vuln\u00e9rables qui tentent de quitter leur pays d\u2019origine en qu\u00eate d\u2019une vie meilleure. Le passage clandestin de personnes est un crime contre un \u00e9tat reposant sur un mouvement, tandis que la traite des personnes est un crime contre un individu reposant sur une exploitation. \n \n Nous limitons l\u2019affichage de sc\u00e8nes de nudit\u00e9 et d\u2019activit\u00e9s sexuelles, car certaines personnes au sein de notre communaut\u00e9 peuvent \u00eatre sensibles \u00e0 ce type de contenu. En outre, nous supprimons par d\u00e9faut les images de nature sexuelle pour emp\u00eacher le partage de contenus montrant des actes non consentis ou des mineurs. Les restrictions sur l\u2019affichage d\u2019activit\u00e9 sexuelle s\u2019appliquent \u00e9galement au contenu cr\u00e9\u00e9 num\u00e9riquement, sauf si le contenu est publi\u00e9 \u00e0 des fins p\u00e9dagogiques, humoristiques ou satiriques. \n\n     Avec le temps, nous avons adapt\u00e9 nos r\u00e8glements relatifs \u00e0 la nudit\u00e9. Nous comprenons que les contenus montrant des sc\u00e8nes de nudit\u00e9 peuvent \u00eatre partag\u00e9s pour diverses raisons, notamment dans le cadre d\u2019une protestation, pour sensibiliser \u00e0 une cause, ou \u00e0 des fins p\u00e9dagogiques ou sanitaires. Par cons\u00e9quent, nous acceptons les contenus respectant de tels motifs. Notre service permet \u00e0 plus de deux\u00a0milliards de personnes de s\u2019exprimer librement, au-del\u00e0 des fronti\u00e8res et des cultures, dans des dizaines de langues. \n     Nous sommes conscients de l\u2019importance pour Facebook d\u2019offrir un espace incitant les gens \u00e0 communiquer, et nous prenons tr\u00e8s au s\u00e9rieux notre r\u00f4le afin d\u2019\u00e9carter les abus de notre service. C\u2019est la raison pour laquelle nous avons  cr\u00e9\u00e9 un ensemble de Standards de la communaut\u00e9  qui expliquent ce qui est autoris\u00e9, ou non, sur Facebook. Nos politiques sont fond\u00e9es sur les retours de notre communaut\u00e9 et l\u2019avis de sp\u00e9cialistes dans des domaines comme les technologies, la s\u00e9curit\u00e9 publique et les droits de l\u2019homme. Pour nous assurer que tout le monde est respect\u00e9, nous nous effor\u00e7ons de cr\u00e9er des politiques qui prennent en compte les diff\u00e9rents points de vue et croyances, surtout ceux des personnes et communaut\u00e9s marginalis\u00e9es ou n\u00e9glig\u00e9es. \n   \n         \n     R\u00c9IT\u00c9RER NOTRE ENGAGEMENT POUR L\u2019EXPRESSION \n     L\u2019objectif de nos Standards de la communaut\u00e9 a toujours \u00e9t\u00e9 de  cr\u00e9er un espace d\u2019expression et de donner une voix aux personnes . Cela n\u2019a pas chang\u00e9 et cela ne changera pas. Pour cr\u00e9er des communaut\u00e9s et rapprocher les gens, il faut pouvoir partager des points de vue, des exp\u00e9riences, des id\u00e9es et des informations vari\u00e9s. Nous souhaitons que les personnes puissent s\u2019exprimer ouvertement sur les sujets qui comptent pour elles, m\u00eame si d\u2019autres peuvent marquer leur d\u00e9saccord ou y trouveraient \u00e0 redire. Dans certains cas, nous autorisons - \u00e0 des fins de sensibilisation - la publication de contenu qui va \u00e0 l\u2019encontre de nos Standards de la communaut\u00e9 s\u2019il est pertinent et d\u2019int\u00e9r\u00eat public. Nous ne prenons cette d\u00e9cision qu\u2019apr\u00e8s avoir \u00e9valu\u00e9 l\u2019impact positif pour l\u2019int\u00e9r\u00eat public par rapport \u00e0 la nuisance potentielle, et nous nous appuyons \u00e0 cet effet sur les principes universels des droits de l\u2019Homme,  tels que mentionn\u00e9s dans notre Politique de l'entreprise en mati\u00e8re de droits de l'Homme . Nous prenons ainsi en consid\u00e9ration l\u2019int\u00e9r\u00eat m\u00e9diatique du contenu publi\u00e9 par tout individu, y compris les agences de presse et les utilisateurs particuliers. Par exemple, nous avons autoris\u00e9 des contenus illustrant graphiquement la guerre ou les cons\u00e9quences de la guerre lorsqu\u2019ils s\u2019av\u00e8rent importants pour la r\u00e9flexion publique.  \n    \n     Notre engagement en faveur de la libert\u00e9 d\u2019expression est primordial, mais nous sommes conscients qu\u2019Internet est une source de formes d\u2019abus nouvelles et croissantes. Lorsque nous limitons la libert\u00e9 d\u2019expression, nous le faisons pour le respect de l\u2019une ou de plusieurs des valeurs suivantes\u00a0: \n   \n       \n\n     Authenticit\u00e9\u00a0:  Nous voulons nous assurer que le contenu que les personnes voient sur Facebook est authentique. Nous sommes convaincus que l\u2019authenticit\u00e9 cr\u00e9e un meilleur environnement pour le partage, et nous ne voulons donc pas que les personnes qui utilisent Facebook mentent sur leur identit\u00e9 ou leurs activit\u00e9s.\n \n    \n    \n      \n    \n     S\u00e9curit\u00e9\u00a0:  Nous nous engageons \u00e0 faire de Facebook un endroit s\u00fbr. Les formes d\u2019expression qui menacent les autres peuvent les intimider, les exclure ou les r\u00e9duire au silence, et ne sont pas autoris\u00e9es sur Facebook. \n  \n    \n  \n    \n    \n     Confidentialit\u00e9\u00a0:  Nous nous engageons \u00e0 prot\u00e9ger votre vie priv\u00e9e et vos informations. La confidentialit\u00e9 donne aux personnes la libert\u00e9 d\u2019\u00eatre elles-m\u00eames, et de choisir quand et comment elles partagent des informations sur Facebook. Cela facilite la cr\u00e9ation de liens.\n \n        \n  \n    \n     Dignit\u00e9\u00a0:  Nous pensons que chacun m\u00e9rite les m\u00eames droits et la m\u00eame dignit\u00e9. Nous attendons de chaque personne qu\u2019elle respecte la dignit\u00e9 d\u2019autrui, et qu\u2019elle ne harc\u00e8le pas et ne rabaisse pas les autres. \n    \n\n\n    \n    \n     Nos Standards de la communaut\u00e9 s\u2019appliquent \u00e0 tout le monde, partout dans le monde, et \u00e0 tous les types de contenu. Ils ont \u00e9t\u00e9 con\u00e7us pour \u00eatre exhaustifs. Par exemple, du contenu qui ne serait pas consid\u00e9r\u00e9 comme haineux pourrait malgr\u00e9 tout \u00eatre supprim\u00e9 parce qu\u2019il enfreint une autre politique. Nous savons que les mots ont diff\u00e9rentes significations et n\u2019affectent pas les personnes de la m\u00eame mani\u00e8re selon leur communaut\u00e9 locale, leur langue et leurs origines. Nous mettons tout en \u0153uvre pour prendre en compte ces nuances tout en appliquant nos politiques de mani\u00e8re juste et coh\u00e9rente pour chaque utilisateur et sa libert\u00e9 d\u2019expression. Notre application de ces standards repose sur les informations dont nous disposons. Dans certains cas, cela signifie qu\u2019il se peut que nous ne d\u00e9tections pas les contenus et les comportements qui volent ces standards, et dans d'autres,  l'application peut \u00eatre limit\u00e9e aux circonstances dans lesquelles nous avons re\u00e7u ce contexte et ces informations suppl\u00e9mentaires. \n\n     Il est possible de signaler du contenu potentiellement en infraction, notamment les Pages, les Groupes, les Profils, le contenu individuel ou des commentaires. Nous les aidons aussi \u00e0 contr\u00f4ler leur propre exp\u00e9rience en leur permettant de  bloquer , de  se d\u00e9sabonner  ou de  masquer  des personnes et des publications.\n       \n\n     La violation de nos Standards de la communaut\u00e9 engendre diverses cons\u00e9quences qui varient en fonction de la gravit\u00e9 de l\u2019infraction et des ant\u00e9c\u00e9dents de la personne sur la plate-forme. Nous pouvons, par exemple, avertir une personne d\u2019une premi\u00e8re infraction, mais si celle-ci persiste \u00e0 enfreindre notre r\u00e8glement, nous pouvons limiter sa capacit\u00e9 \u00e0 publier du contenu sur Facebook ou d\u00e9sactiver son profil. Lorsque nous pensons qu\u2019un contenu repr\u00e9sente un r\u00e9el risque de pr\u00e9judice physique ou une atteinte directe \u00e0 la s\u00e9curit\u00e9 publique, nous pouvons \u00e9galement en informer les autorit\u00e9s. \n     Nos Standards de la communaut\u00e9 d\u00e9finissent ce qui est autoris\u00e9 ou non sur Facebook.   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n  Threats that could lead to death (and other forms of high-severity violence) targeting people or places where threat is defined as any of the following:\n\n      \n              Statements of intent to commit high-severity violence. This includes content where a symbol represents the target and\/or includes a visual of an armament or method to represent violence. \n        Calls for high-severity violence including content where no target is specified but a symbol represents the target and\/or includes a visual of an armament or method that represents violence. \n        Statements advocating for high-severity violence. \n        Aspirational or conditional statements to commit high-severity violence. \n     \n      \n      Content that asks or offers services for hire to kill others (for example, hitmen, mercenaries, assassins) or advocates for the use of a hitman, mercenary or assassin against a target \n     \n      Admissions, statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to kidnap a target \n      Content that depicts abductions or kidnappings if it is clear the content is not being shared by a victim or their family as a plea for help, or shared for informational, condemnation or awareness raising purposes \n\nThreats of high-severity violence using digitally-produced or altered imagery to target living people with armaments, methods of violence or dismemberment\n \n   Threats that lead to serious injury (mid-severity violence) toward private individuals, unnamed specified persons, minor public figures, high-risk persons or high-risk groups where threat is defined as any of the following:\n\n      \n Statements of intent to commit violence, or \n        Statements advocating violence, or \n        Calls for mid-severity violence including content where no target is specified but a symbol represents the target, or \n        Aspirational or conditional statements to commit violence, or  \n   Content about other target(s) apart from private individuals, minor public figures, high-risk persons or high-risk groups and any credible:\n      \n     \n          Statements of intent to commit violence, or \n          Calls for action of violence, or \n          Statements advocating for violence, or \n       Aspirational or conditional statements to commit violence \n   \n    \n\n      Threats that lead to physical harm (or other forms of lower-severity violence) towards private individuals (self-reporting required) or minor public figures where threat is defined as any of the following:\n         \n      \n            Private individuals (name and\/or face match are required) or minor public figures that includes:\n          \n       \n                Statements of intent, calls for action, advocating, aspirational or conditional statements to commit low-severity violence  \n              \n      \n    \n     Any content created for the express purpose of outing an individual as a member of a designated and recognisable at-risk group\n \n        Instructions on how to make or use weapons if there is evidence of a goal to seriously injure or kill people through:\n     \n          \n            Language explicitly stating that goal, or \n            Photos or videos that show or simulate the end result (serious injury or death) as part of the instruction. \n            Unless the aforementioned content is shared as part of recreational self defense, for military training purposes, commercial video games, or news coverage (posted by a Page or with a news logo). \n          \n      \n     \n      Providing instructions on how to make or use explosives, unless there is clear context that the content is for a non-violent purpose (for example, part of commercial video games, clear scientific\/educational purpose, fireworks or specifically for fishing)\n       \n      \n   Any content containing statements of intent, calls for action, conditional or aspirational statements, or advocating for violence due to voting, voter registration or the administration or outcome of an election \n\n      Statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to bring weapons  to locations, including but not limited to places of worship, educational facilities, polling places or locations used to count votes or administer an election (or encouraging others to do the same). \n     \n\n \n  \n  \n \n       For the following Community Standards, we require additional information and\/or context to enforce:  \n\n\n     \n\n      \n       Do not post: \n  \n    Content that puts LGBTQI+ people at risk by revealing their sexual identity against their will or without permission. \n Content that puts unveiled women at risk by revealing their images without veil against their will or without permission. \n    Violent threats against law enforcement officers. \n    Violent threats against people accused of a crime. We remove this content when we have reason to believe that the content is intended to cause physical harm. \n    Misinformation and unverifiable rumors that contribute to the risk of imminent violence or physical harm.\n        \n   \n      \n   \n   \n     Additionally, we have specific rules and guidance regarding content related to COVID-19 and vaccines. To see these specific rules please click  here. \n   \n     \n Coded statements where the method of violence or harm is not clearly articulated, but the threat is veiled or implicit. Facebook looks at the below signals to determine whether there is a threat of harm in the content.\n   \n     \n         Shared in a retaliatory context (e.g., expressions of desire to do something harmful to others in response to a grievance or threat that may be real, perceived or anticipated) \n References to historical or fictional incidents of violence (e.g., content that threatens others by referring to known historical incidents of violence that have been executed throughout history or in fictional settings) \n Acts as a threatening call-to-action (e.g. content inviting or encouraging others to carry out harmful acts or to join in carrying out the harmful acts) \n Indicates knowledge of or shares sensitive information that could expose others to harm (e.g. content that either makes note of or implies awareness of personal information that might make a threat of physical violence more credible. This includes implying knowledge of a person's residential address, their place of employment or education, daily commute routes or current location) \n Local context or subject matter expertise confirms that the statement in question could be threatening and\/or could lead to imminent violence or physical harm. \n     The subject of the threat reports the content to us.   \n\n \n    Threats against election officials \n    Implicit statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to bring armaments to locations, including but not limited to places of worship, educational facilities, polling places, or locations used to count votes or administer an election (or encouraging others to do the same). We may also restrict calls to bring armaments to certain locations where there are temporarily signals of a heightened risk of violence or offline harm. This may be the case, for example, when there is a known protest and counter-protest planned or violence broke out at a protest in the same city within the last 7 days   \n   \n      \n      \n      \n      \n       \n\n     \n  \n\n     \n         \n    \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   We aim to prevent potential offline harm that may be related to content on Facebook. While we understand that people commonly express disdain or disagreement by threatening or calling for violence in non-serious ways, we remove language that incites or facilitates serious violence. We remove content, disable accounts and work with law enforcement when we believe there is a genuine risk of physical harm or direct threats to public safety. We also try to consider the language and context in order to distinguish casual statements from content that constitutes a credible threat to public or personal safety. In determining whether a threat is credible, we may also consider additional information like a person's public visibility and the risks to their physical safety. \n  \n     In some cases, we see written or verbal admissions of engagement in self injury, including: \n    \n    \n      Suicide. \n      Euthanasia\/assisted suicide. \n      Self-harm. \n      Eating disorders. \n    \n     \n     \n     \n     \n       \n  \n\n  \n    For the following Community Standards, we require additional information and\/or context to enforce:  \n    \n     \n     We may remove suicide notes when we have confirmation of a suicide or suicide attempt. We try to identify suicide notes using several factors, including but not limited to, family or legal representative requests, media reports, law enforcement reports or other third party sources (e.g. government agencies, NGOs).\n     \n       A suicide note may also be removed when reported through the   Suicidal Content Contact Form   or  Instagram Contact Form  when we have confirmation of a suicide or suicide attempt \n       \n    \n  \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   We care deeply about the safety of the people who use our apps. We regularly consult with experts in suicide and self-injury to help inform our policies and enforcement, and work with organizations around the world to provide assistance to people in distress.\n     \nWhile we do not allow people to intentionally or unintentionally celebrate or promote suicide or self-injury, we do allow people to discuss these topics because we want Facebook to be a space where people can share their experiences, raise awareness about these issues, and seek support from one another.\n  \nWe define self-injury as the intentional and direct injuring of the body, including self-mutilation and eating disorders. We remove any content that encourages suicide or self-injury, including fictional content such as memes or illustrations and any self-injury content which is graphic, regardless of context. We also remove content that identifies and negatively targets victims or survivors of suicide or self-injury seriously, humorously or rhetorically, as well as real time depictions of suicide or self-injury. Content about recovery of suicide or self-harm that is allowed, but may contain imagery that could be upsetting, such as a healed scar, is placed behind a sensitivity screen.\n  \nWhen people post or search for suicide or self-injury- related content, we will direct them to local organizations that can provide support and if someone is at immediate risk of harming themselves, we will contact local emergency services to get them help.\n  \nWith respect to live content, experts have told us that if someone is saying they intend to attempt suicide on a livestream, we should leave the content up for as long as possible, because the longer someone is talking to a camera, the more opportunity there is for a friend or family member to call emergency services.\n  \nHowever, to minimize the risk of others being negatively impacted by viewing this content, we will stop the livestream at the point at which the threat turns into an attempt. As mentioned above, in any case, we will contact emergency services if we identify someone is at immediate risk of harming themselves.\n  \n     \n \n We do not tolerate this kind of behavior because it prevents people from feeling safe and respected on Facebook.  \n\n We distinguish between public figures and private individuals because we want to allow discussion, which often includes critical commentary of people who are featured in the news or who have a large public audience. For public figures, we remove attacks that are severe as well as certain attacks where the public figure is directly tagged in the post or comment.  \n  \n   For private individuals, our protection goes further: We remove content that's meant to degrade or shame, including, for example, claims about someone's sexual activity. We recognize that bullying and harassment can have more of an emotional impact on minors, which is why our policies provide heightened protection for users between the ages of 13 and 18. \n\n Context and intent matter, and we allow people to post and share if it is clear that something was shared in order to condemn or draw attention to bullying and harassment. In certain instances, we require self-reporting because it helps us understand that the person targeted feels bullied or harassed. In addition to reporting such behavior and content, we encourage people to use  tools available on Facebook  to help protect against it. \n    \n     We also have a  Bullying Prevention Hub , which is a resource for teens, parents, and educators seeking support for issues related to bullying and other conflicts. It offers step-by-step guidance, including information on how to start important conversations about bullying. Learn more about what we are doing to protect people from bullying and harassment  here . \n   \n "},"human_exploitation":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n      Content or exhibited behavior that may lead to human exploitation, which includes any of the following:\n\n      \n        Sex trafficking, covering minors and adults. \n        The sale of children for illegal adoption.\n         \n        Orphanage trafficking and orphanage volun-tourism.\n           \n        Forced marriages.\n         \n        Labor exploitation (including bonded labor).\n         \n        Domestic servitude.\n         \n        Non-regenerative organ trafficking. \n        Forced criminal activity (e.g. forced begging, forced drug trafficking). \n        Recruitment of child soldiers. \n           \n\n      Content geared towards the:\n      \n        Recruitment of potential victims through force, fraud, coercion, enticement, deception, blackmail or other non-consensual acts. \n        Facilitation of human exploitation by coordinating, transporting, transferring, harboring or brokering of victims prior or during the exploitation.  \n        Exploitation of humans by promoting, depicting or advocating for it. \n        \n      Content that offers or assists in smuggling of humans \n      \n         \n    \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   After consulting with outside experts from around the world, we are consolidating several existing exploitation policies, that were previously housed in different sections of the Community Standards into one dedicated section that focuses on human exploitation and captures a broad range of harmful activities that may manifest on our platform. Experts think and talk about these issues under one umbrella human exploitation.   \n     \n     \n     \n      In an effort to disrupt and prevent harm, we remove content that facilitates or coordinates the exploitation of humans, including human trafficking. We define human trafficking as the business of depriving someone of liberty for profit. It is the exploitation of humans in order to force them to engage   in commercial sex, labor or other activities against their will. It relies on deception, force and coercion, and degrades humans by depriving them of their freedom while economically or materially benefiting others.   \n     \n     \n     \n      Human trafficking is multi-faceted and global; it can affect anyone regardless of age, socioeconomic background, ethnicity, gender or location. It takes many forms, and any given trafficking situation can involve various stages of development. By the coercive nature of this abuse, victims cannot consent. \n     \n     \n     \n      While we need to be careful not to conflate human trafficking and smuggling, they can be related and exhibit overlap. The United Nations defines human smuggling as the procurement or facilitation of illegal entry into a state across international borders. Without necessity for coercion or force, it may still result in the exploitation of vulnerable individuals who are trying to leave their country of origin, often in pursuit of a better life. Human smuggling is a crime against a state, relying on movement, and human trafficking is a crime against a person, relying on exploitation. \n \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   We believe that people use their voice and connect more freely when they don\u2019t feel attacked on the basis of who they are. That is why we don\u2019t allow hate speech on Facebook. It creates an environment of intimidation and exclusion, and in some cases may promote offline violence. \n\n     We define hate speech as a direct attack against people on the basis of what we call protected characteristics: race, ethnicity, national origin, disability, religious affiliation, caste, sexual orientation, sex, gender identity and serious disease.  We define attacks as violent or dehumanizing speech, harmful stereotypes, statements of inferiority, expressions of contempt, disgust or dismissal, cursing and calls for exclusion or segregation. We consider age a protected characteristic when referenced along with another protected characteristic. We also protect refugees, migrants, immigrants and asylum seekers from the most severe attacks, though we do allow commentary and criticism of immigration policies. Similarly, we provide some protections for characteristics like occupation, when they\u2019re referenced along with a protected characteristic. \n    \n    \n     We recognize that people sometimes share content that includes someone else\u2019s hate speech to condemn it or raise awareness. In other cases, speech that might otherwise violate our standards can be used self-referentially or in an empowering way. Our policies are designed to allow room for these types of speech, but we require people to clearly indicate their intent. If the intention is unclear, we may remove content. \n    \n\n     Learn more about our approach to hate speech.\n   \n \n "},"graphic_violence":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n      Imagery of people   \n Videos of people or dead bodies in non-medical settings if they depict\n   \n  \t Dismemberment. \n     Visible internal organs; partially decomposed bodies. \n     Charred or burning people unless in the context of cremation or self-immolation when that action is a form of political speech or newsworthy. \n     Victims of cannibalism. \n     Throat-slitting. \n        \n \n      Live streams of capital punishment of a person \n\n     \n    \n  \n   \n      \n  For the following content, we include a warning screen so that people are aware the content may be disturbing. because it may create an environment that discourages participation. We allow graphic content (with some limitations) to help people raise awareness about these issues.  \n    \n    We know that people value the ability to discuss important issues like human rights abuses or acts of terrorism. We are a service for more than two billion people to freely express themselves across countries and cultures and in dozens of languages. \n     We recognize how important it is for Facebook to be a place where people feel empowered to communicate, and we take seriously our role in keeping abuse off our service. That\u2019s why we\u2019ve  developed a set of Community Standards  that outline what is and is not allowed on Facebook. Our policies are based on feedback from our community and the advice of experts in fields such as technology, public safety and human rights. To ensure that everyone\u2019s voice is valued, we take great care to craft policies that are inclusive of different views and beliefs, in particular those of people and communities that might otherwise be overlooked or marginalized. \n   \n         \n     REITERATING OUR COMMITMENT TO VOICE \n     The goal of our Community Standards has always been to  create a place for expression and give people a voice . This has not and will not change. Building community and bringing the world closer together depends on people\u2019s ability to share diverse views, experiences, ideas and information. We want people to be able to talk openly about the issues that matter to them, even if some may disagree or find them objectionable. In some cases, we allow content for public awareness which would otherwise go against our Community Standards \u2013 if it is newsworthy and in the public interest. We do this only after weighing the public interest value against the risk of harm and we look to international human rights standards,  as reflected in our Corporate Human Rights Policy,   to make these judgments. As such, we consider the newsworthiness of content posted by anyone, including news organizations and individuals users. For example, we have allowed content that graphically depicts war or the consequences of war where it is important to public discourse.  \n    \n     Our commitment to expression is paramount, but we recognize the internet creates new and increased opportunities for abuse. For these reasons, when we limit expression, we do it in service of one or more of the following values: \n   \n       \n\n     Authenticity:  We want to make sure the content people are seeing on Facebook is authentic. We believe that authenticity creates a better environment for sharing, and that\u2019s why we don\u2019t want people using Facebook to misrepresent who they are or what they\u2019re doing.\n \n    \n    \n      \n    \n     Safety:  We are committed to making Facebook a safe place. Expression that threatens people has the potential to intimidate, exclude or silence others and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook. \n  \n    \n  \n    \n    \n     Privacy:  We are committed to protecting personal privacy and information. Privacy gives people the freedom to be themselves, and to choose how and when to share on Facebook and to connect more easily.\n \n        \n  \n    \n     Dignity:  We believe that all people are equal in dignity and rights. We expect that people will respect the dignity of others and not harass or degrade others. \n    \n\n\n    \n    \n     Our Community Standards apply to everyone, all around the world, and to all types of content. They\u2019re designed to be comprehensive \u2013 for example, content that might not be considered hateful may still be removed for violating a different policy. We recognize that words mean different things or affect people differently depending on their local community, language, or background. We work hard to account for these nuances while also applying our policies consistently and fairly to people and their expression. Our enforcement of these standards relies on information available to us. In some cases, this means that we may not detect content and behavior that violates these standards, and in others,  enforcement may be limited to circumstances where we have been provided with additional information and context. \n\n     People can report potentially violating content, including Pages, Groups, Profiles, individual content, and comments. We also may notify law enforcement when we believe there is a genuine risk of physical harm or a direct threat to public safety. \n     Our Community Standards are a guide for what is and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook.
